Changelog

2024/10/01

Breaking: field and enums

  • Field m365DayToDayModeBackupStats was removed from Query type.
  • Cluster.cyberEventLockdownSupportCaseDetails field type changed from CyberEventLockdownSupportCaseDetails! to CyberEventLockdownSupportCaseDetails.
  • CascadingArchivalSpec.archivalLocationToClusterMapping field type changed from [ArchivalLocationToClusterMapping!] to [CascadingArchivalLocationToClusterMapping!].

Breaking: types

  • DayToDayModeBackupStats type was removed.
  • Input field invalidateAllSessions was added to ResetUsersPasswordsWithUserIdsInput type.

Deprecations

  • Field mongodbSources was deprecated in Query type.

    Reason: Use mongoSources instead. Scheduled for removal after 2025/09/03.

  • Field mongodbCollections was deprecated in Query type.

    Reason: Use mongoCollections instead. Scheduled for removal after 2025/09/03.

  • Field updateMongodbSource was deprecated in Mutation type.

    Reason: Use patchMongoSource instead. Scheduled for removal after 2025/09/03.

  • Field bulkDeleteMongodbSources was deprecated in Mutation type.

    Reason: Use bulkDeleteMongoSources instead. Scheduled for removal after 2025/09/03.

  • Field createMongodbSource was deprecated in Mutation type.

    Reason: Use addMongoSource instead. Scheduled for removal after 2025/09/03.

  • Field mongodbCollectionRecoverableRange was deprecated in Query type.

    Reason: Use mongoRecoverableRanges instead. Scheduled for removal after 2025/09/03.

  • Field mongodbCollection was deprecated in Query type.

    Reason: Use mongoCollection instead. Scheduled for removal after 2025/09/03.

  • Field mongodbSource was deprecated in Query type.

    Reason: Use mongoSource instead. Scheduled for removal after 2025/09/03.

  • Field deleteMongodbSource was deprecated in Mutation type.

    Reason: Use deleteMongoSource instead. Scheduled for removal after 2025/09/03.

  • Field mongodbDatabase was deprecated in Query type.

    Reason: Use mongoDatabase instead. Scheduled for removal after 2025/09/03.

  • Field mongodbBulkRecoverableRange was deprecated in Query type.

    Reason: Use mongoBulkRecoverableRanges instead. Scheduled for removal after 2025/09/03.

  • Field recoverMongodbSource was deprecated in Mutation type.

    Reason: Use recoverMongoSource instead. Scheduled for removal after 2025/09/03.

  • Field mongodbDatabases was deprecated in Query type.

    Reason: Use mongoDatabases instead. Scheduled for removal after 2025/09/03.

2024/09/01

Breaking: field and enums

  • Input field feedId was removed from DeleteIntelFeedInput type.
  • Mutation.deleteIntelFeed field type changed from DeleteIntelFeedReply! to Void.
  • LicenseConsumptionType.fetbConsumed field type changed from Long! to Long.
  • Mutation.updateCustomIntelFeed field type changed from UpdateCustomIntelFeedReply! to Void.
  • LicenseConsumptionType.usersProtected field type changed from Int! to Int.

Breaking: types

  • DeleteIntelFeedReply type was removed.
  • UpdateCustomIntelFeedReply type was removed.
  • M365Snapshot type was removed.

Deprecations

  • Field aggregateClusterHealth was deprecated in ClusterConnection type.

Reason: This field is deprecated because it is no longer used. Scheduled for removal after 2025/07/29.

  • Field objectId was deprecated in RbacObject type.

Reason: Deprecated: use managedId instead. Scheduled for removal after 2025/08/12.

  • SlaReplicationPair.sourceCluster field type changed from UUID! to SlaDataLocationCluster!.
  • SlaReplicationPair.targetCluster field type changed from UUID! to SlaDataLocationCluster!.
  • ListM365DirectoryObjectAttributesInput.orgId input field type changed from String to UUID!.
  • ListM365DirectoryObjectAttributesInput.attributeType input field type changed from AttributeType to AttributeType!.
  • ListM365DirectoryObjectAttributesInput.objectType input field type changed from DirectoryObjectType to DirectoryObjectType!.

Breaking: types

  • PhysicalHost object type no longer implements MongoSourcePhysicalChildType interface.
  • Input field maxResults was added to ListM365DirectoryObjectAttributesInput type.
  • PhysicalHost object type no longer implements MongoSourceDescendantType interface.
  • Input field kmsKeyVaultId was added to AzureKeyVaultKeyIdentifierInput type.
  • Query.decryptExportUrl(workloadFid) type changed from UUID to UUID!.

Deprecations

  • Field dataHosts was deprecated in MongoSource type.

Reason: Use hostDetails instead. Scheduled for removal after 2025/07/30.

  • Field cloudAccountId was deprecated in CcWithCloudInfo type.

Reason: This field is deprecated because it is no longer used. Scheduled for removal after 2025/07/30.

2024/04/01

Breaking: field and enums

  • Field snapshotId was removed from ActiveDirectorySearchVersions type.
  • ApplicationCloudAccountToExocomputeConfig.exocomputeConfigs field type changed from AwsExocomputeGetConfigurationResponse to [AwsExocomputeGetConfigurationResponse!]!.
  • AccountProduct.expirationDate field type changed from DateTime! to DateTime.
  • ActiveDirectorySnappableSearchResponse.versions field type changed from ActiveDirectorySearchVersions! to [ActiveDirectorySearchVersions!]!.

Breaking: types

  • Argument permissionsGroups was added to Query.azureCloudAccountPermissionConfig field.

Deprecations

  • Field vsphereVMRecoverableRange was deprecated in Query type.

Reason: Deprecated. Use vmwareRecoverableRanges instead. Scheduled for removal after 2025/03/05.

  • Field vsphereVMMissedRecoverableRange was deprecated in Query type.

Reason: Deprecated. Use vmwareVmMissedRecoverableRange instead. Scheduled for removal after 2025/03/05.

2023/11/01

Breaking: field and enums

  • Field physicalChildConnection was removed from ManagedVolumeMount type.
  • Field active was removed from PasswordComplexityPolicyTemplate type.
  • Field descendantConnection was removed from ManagedVolumeMount type.
  • Enum value JIRA_PROJECT_KEY was removed from enum HierarchyFilterField.
  • NutanixVmMountSummary.mountStatus field type changed from String to NutanixVmMountStatus.

Breaking: types

  • ManagedVolumeMountDescendantTypeConnection type was removed.
  • ManagedVolumeMountPhysicalChildTypeEdge type was removed.
  • ManagedVolumeMountPhysicalChildType type was removed.
  • ManagedVolumeMountPhysicalChildTypeConnection type was removed.
  • ManagedVolumeMountDescendantTypeEdge type was removed.
  • ManagedVolumeMountDescendantType type was removed.
  • PhysicalHost object type no longer implements ManagedVolumeMountDescendantType interface.
  • PhysicalHost object type no longer implements ManagedVolumeDescendantType interface.
  • PhysicalHost object type no longer implements ManagedVolumeMountPhysicalChildType interface.

Deprecations

  • Field orgName was deprecated in TaskDetail type.

Reason: taskOrg field captures the basic org details. Scheduled for removal after 2024/11/02.

  • Field orgName was deprecated in Snappable type.

Reason: snappableOrg field captures the basic org details. Scheduled for removal after 2024/11/02.

  • Field vsphereVmRecoverFiles was deprecated in Mutation type.

Reason: Deprecated. Use vsphereVmRecoverFilesNew instead. Scheduled for removal after 2024/09/27.

  • Field vsphereExcludeVmDisks was deprecated in Mutation type.

Reason: Deprecated. Use excludeVmDisks instead. Scheduled for removal after 2024/09/27.

2023/10/01

Breaking: field and enums

  • Field deleteFailedClusterOperationJobData was removed from Mutation type.
  • Input field accountId was removed from UnmountDiskInput type.
  • Input field mountDiskIds was removed from UnmountDiskInput type.
  • Input field accountId was removed from MountDiskInput type.
  • Input field mountId was removed from UnmountDiskInput type.
  • Enum value PAST_90_DAYS was removed from enum PastDurationEnum.
  • Enum value START_OF_PROTECTION was removed from enum PastDurationEnum.
  • Mutation.unmountDisk field type changed from AsyncJobStatus! to Void.
  • Mutation.mountDisk field type changed from AsyncJobStatus! to MountDiskReply!.
  • MountDiskInput.snapshotType input field type changed from SnapshotType to SnapshotType!.
  • DeleteCsrInput.csrFids input field type changed from [UUID!] to [UUID!]!.
  • GetCsrInput.csrFid input field type changed from UUID to UUID!.

Breaking: types

  • DeleteFailedClusterOperationJobDataInput type was removed.
  • DeleteFailedClusterOperationJobDataReply type was removed.
  • VsphereDatacenter object type no longer implements VsphereFolderLogicalChildType interface.
  • Input field targetWorkloadId was added to UnmountDiskInput type.
  • Input field mountIds was added to UnmountDiskInput type.
  • Input field liveMountId was added to UnmountDiskInput type.
  • VsphereDatacenter object type no longer implements VsphereFolderDescendantType interface.
  • Input field workloadType was added to MountDiskInput type.
  • Argument featuresWithPermissionsGroups was added to Query.allLatestFeaturePermissionsForCloudAccounts field.

2023/09/01

Breaking: field and enums

  • Input field roleCustomization was removed from ValidateAndCreateAwsCloudAccountInput type.
  • Input field name was removed from AwsNativeAccountInput type.
  • Enum value SAAS_APPS_OBJECT_TYPE was removed from enum SlaObjectType.
  • DlpConfig.policies field type changed from [String!]! to [String!].

Breaking: types

  • Argument features was removed from Query.allAwsPermissionPolicies field.
  • Argument awsCloudType was removed from Query.allAwsPermissionPolicies field.
  • Argument userAccessObjectsFilter was added to Query.policyObjs field.
  • Argument input was added to Query.allAwsPermissionPolicies field.

Deprecations

  • Field host was deprecated in SapHanaHostObject type.

Reason: Use systemHost instead. Scheduled for removal after 2024/07/28.

Deprecations

  • Field mappedCloudAccountIds was deprecated in AwsExocomputeConfig type.

Reason: Use mappedCloudAccounts instead, cloud account IDs of mapped accounts are contained in mappedCloudAccounts. Scheduled for removal after 2024/06/27.

  • Field mappedCloudAccountIds was deprecated in AzureSubscriptionWithExoConfigs type.

Reason: Use mappedCloudAccounts instead. The cloud account IDs of the mapped accounts are contained in the field 'mappedCloudAccounts'. Scheduled for removal after 2024/06/27.

  • Field allOrgsWithAccess was deprecated in GlobalSlaReply type.

Reason: This field is deprecated and has been replaced by the allOrgsHavingAccess field, which must be used instead. Scheduled for removal after 2024/06/27.

  • Field isPactsafeEnabled was deprecated in EulaState type.

Reason: Use isPactsafeV2Enabled instead. Scheduled for removal after 2024/06/27.

Reason: Use pactsafeEulaState instead. Scheduled for removal after 2024/06/27.

2023/02/01

Breaking: field and enums

  • Field createConfigProtectionSetup was removed from Mutation type.
  • Field updateConfigProtectionSetup was removed from Mutation type.
  • RcvEntitlementsUsageDetails.entitlement field type changed from RcvEntitlement! to RcvEntitlement.
  • RcvAccountEntitlement.entitlements field type changed from RcvEntitlementsUsageDetails to [RcvEntitlementsUsageDetails!]!.
  • SnapshotFile.workloadFields field type changed from WorkloadFields! to WorkloadFields.
  • O365SnapshotItemInfo.id field type changed from UUID! to String!.
  • O365SnapshotItemInfo.parentFolderId field type changed from UUID to String.

Breaking: types

  • CreateConfigProtectionSetupInput type was removed.
  • UpdateConfigProtectionSetupInput type was removed.
  • ConfigProtectionCaCert type was removed.
  • Input field shouldRunAsynchronously was added to BulkRefreshHostsInput type.

Deprecations

  • Field snapshotFilesDelta was deprecated in Query type.

Reason: This endpoint only works for Data Center workloads. Use snapshotFilesDeltaV2 instead. Scheduled for removal after 2024/01/31.
